data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="heading.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><h1 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Welcome to the Kizomba Embassy!</h1></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-151b4b0 animated-slow elementor-widget-divider--view-line elementor-widget elementor-widget-divider" data-id="151b4b0" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="divider.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-divider">
<span class="elementor-divider-separator">
</span></div></div></div></div></div><div class="has_eae_slider elementor-column elementor-col-33 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-775de24 elementor-hidden-phone" data-eae-slider="12686" data-id="775de24" data-element_type="column" data-settings="{&quot;animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}"><div class="elementor-widget-wrap"></div></div></div></section><section class="has_eae_slider elementor-section elementor-inner-section elementor-element elementor-element-5415cda elementor-section-boxed elementor-section-height-default elementor-section-height-default" data-eae-slider="70486" data-id="5415cda" data-element_type="section" data-settings="{&quot;animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;,&quot;background_background&quot;:&quot;classic&quot;}"><div class="elementor-background-overlay"></div><div class="elementor-container elementor-column-gap-default"><div class="has_eae_slider elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-2c614c4" data-eae-slider="3374" data-id="2c614c4" data-element_type="column" data-settings="{&quot;animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}"><div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated"><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-e07a2ef animated-slow elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="e07a2ef" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><p>This is an organization dedicated to growing the community. Indeed we do this by highlighting all styles of professional kizomba dance instructors, festivals, and events worldwide! Moreover, this includes Semba, Urban Kiz, and Kiz Fusion.</p><p>Specifically, it is a popular genre of music and dance originating in Angola circa 1984. It means party in Kimbundu, a Bantu language spoken by the Ambundu or Mbundu of Angola.</p><p>Additionally, this type of music was developed by musicians who were influenced by semba music and zouk music from the Caribbean French Antilles. </p><p>Meanwhile, the dance roots come from Semba. To illustrate, it was traditionally danced in a circular pattern, whereas Urban Kiz is danced in a straight line. Kiz Fusion has more flexible rules and includes moves and techniques from other dance styles. </p></div></div><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-dec3547 animated-slow elementor-hidden-phone elementor-widget elementor-widget-button" data-id="dec3547" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="button.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container"><div class="elementor-button-wrapper">

</span>
</a></div></div></div></div></div><div class="has_eae_slider elementor-column elementor-col-50 elementor-inner-column elementor-element elementor-element-1aaf044" data-eae-slider="79596" data-id="1aaf044" data-element_type="column" data-settings="{&quot;animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}"><div class="elementor-widget-wrap elementor-element-populated"><div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0cc4d06 animated-slow elementor-widget elementor-widget-image" data-id="0cc4d06" data-element_type="widget" data-settings="{&quot;_animation&quot;:&quot;none&quot;}" data-widget_type="image.default"><div class="elementor-widget-container">
